<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijklank.html>bijklank</a> (84746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bijou.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijou.html>bijou</a> (25445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijou.html>bijou</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Breton language"><a href = vnd.unilang:breton.html>Breton</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="br">bizoù</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnenband.html>binnenband</a> (95155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnenband.html>binnenband</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnenband.html>binnenbanden</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:binnenband.html>binnenbandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
